[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A Jazzer fuzzing run against the Apache POI POIFSDump tool triggered a critical     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         security exception indicating a file path traversal vulnerability. The fuzzer’s     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         input caused the code to construct or resolve a pathname that escapes an intended   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         directory, leading to the detection of an unauthorized traversal outside the        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         designated output location.                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Issue Type                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           The exception raised is                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         traversal`. This indicates that untrusted input was used to manipulate file paths,  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         allowing directory traversal beyond a permitted root.                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Vulnerability Characteristics                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The sanitizer in `FilePathTraversal.check` detected an input path containing    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `..[35m/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`, which navigates above the sandboxed directory.      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • This points to a file path traversal vulnerability, where crafted filenames or  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         paths can break out of constrained directories and access or overwrite arbitrary    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         filesystem locations.                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Key Observations                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The exception originates in                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook`, which [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         hooks the first path argument when a file operation is invoked.                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The fuzzer target is `org.apache.poi.poifs.dev.POIFSDump.dump` [1m([0mcalled from     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `POIFSDump.main`[1m)[0m, exercised via `POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`.           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The failing input name `q/r/s/t/input.bin_dump/Root                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Entry/..[35m/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m` demonstrates nested directories plus            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         back-references [1m([0m`..[35m/[0m`[1m)[0m to break confinement.                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Affected Code Areas for Investigation                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • File argument handling in `POIFSDump.dump` and any code that constructs or      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         normalizes output paths.                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • Entry point logic in `POIFSDump.main` where output directories or filenames are [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         determined.                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • Path sanitization and resolution routines [1m([0me.g., calls to `java.io.File`,       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `java.nio.file.Path`, or custom normalization[1m)[0m within the POI dump utility.         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • Integration with the Jazzer harness [1m([0m`POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer`[1m)[0m, to confirm how the  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         file paths are passed to the target code.                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         By reviewing these areas, one can understand how untrusted or fuzz-controlled path  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         segments bypass intended directory restrictions and trigger a traversal scenario.   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         parent directory, and creating necessary directories. After applying the patch, the [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         build fails with two compilation errors in `POIFSDump.java`, reporting an unmatched [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `else` and a misplaced closing brace.                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. Initial Issue                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - During fuzz testing of `POIFSDump`, Jazzer raised a critical security issue:   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              `File path traversal: [33m...[0m[35m/[0m[95mRoot[0m Entry/..[35m/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`.            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - This indicates that POIFSDump uses archive entry names directly to construct   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         output file paths, allowing `..` segments or separators to escape the target        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         directory.                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Important Observations                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The exception originates in the Jazzer sanitizer                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`FilePathTraversal.checkPath`[1m)[0m, not inside POI logic.                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The vulnerable code is in `org.apache.poi.poifs.dev.POIFSDump.dump`, which     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         iterates over `Entry` objects and writes data to `new [1;35mFile[0m[1m([0mparent,                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mentry.getName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m` without sanitization.                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Both `DocumentEntry` [1m([0mfiles[1m)[0m and `DirectoryEntry` [1m([0msubdirectories[1m)[0m are handled [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         similarly, but only the latter has manual `mkdirs` support.                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Patch Attempt                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Imported `java.nio.file.Path`.                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - In the branch handling file entries, replaced `new [1;35mFile[0m[1m([0mparent,                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mentry.getName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m` with:                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Trim and replace `..` and separators in the raw entry name.                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Construct `outPath` via `[1;35m.toPath[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Verify `[1;35moutPath.startsWith[0m[1m([0mparentPath[1m)[0m`.                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Create parent directories with `Files.createDirectories`.                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Write bytes via `[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1m([0moutPath[1m)[0m`.                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - In the branch handling directory entries, applied analogous sanitization,      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         normalization, prefix checks, and `[1;35mmkdirs[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. Patch Result and Build Output                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Compilation errors in `POIFSDump.java`:                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • “`else` without `if`” at line [1;36m136[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • “class, interface, or enum expected” at line [1;36m157[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The errors indicate mismatched braces or control-flow structure introduced by  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the patch. The new `else if [1m([0mentry instanceof DirectoryEntry[1m)[0m` appears outside any  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         preceding `if` block, and a closing brace was placed incorrectly, leaving the class [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         body unbalanced.                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m. Code Areas for Further Investigation                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The `[1;35mdump[0m[1m([0mDirectoryEntry, File[1m)[0m` and `[1;35mdump[0m[1m([0mPOIFSFileSystem, …[1m)[0m` overloads in   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `POIFSDump.java` to ensure all entry-writing paths are sanitized.                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Control-flow and brace matching within the `dump` method to restore syntactic  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         correctness.                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Handling of both `DocumentEntry` and `DirectoryEntry` to apply consistent name [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         sanitization.                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Any duplicated or outdated overloads of `dump` that may have been partially    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         removed or commented out during the patch.                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Initial Issue Log                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Here is the initial issue log of the codebase:                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m<[0m[1;95missue[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         == libFuzzer crashing input ==                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         An OSS-Fuzz run on Apache POI’s `POIFSDump` tool triggered a Jazzer security        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         sanitizer error reporting a file path traversal vulnerability. The fuzzer supplied  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         a crafted POIFS entry name containing `..[35m/[0m` sequences, which `POIFSDump` wrote      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         directly to disk under `[35m/[0m[95mtmp[0m`, allowing escape from the intended output directory.  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         To mitigate, a patch was applied to `POIFSDump.java` that:                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Introduces filename sanitization by replacing `..` and path separators in entry   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         names.                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Normalizes and bounds-checks output paths against the parent directory.           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Applies the same pattern to both file entries and directory entries.              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Extends the static overload of `[1;35mdump[0m[1m([0mPOIFSFileSystem,…[1m)[0m` with equivalent          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         sanitization logic.                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         After applying the patch, the build fails with a series of “illegal start of        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         expression” and related syntax errors, all pointing to the `public static void      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mdump[0m[1m([0mPOIFSFileSystem …[1m)[0m` method declaration. The errors indicate that the method    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         signature was encountered in an unexpected location, likely due to mismatched or    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         missing braces in the surrounding code.                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. Initial Issue                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - A Jazzer fuzzer invocation in `POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         exercised `POIFSDump.main`, causing a `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer to trigger on a [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         path containing `..[35m/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`.                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The underlying code in `[1;35mPOIFSDump.dump[0m[1m([0mDirectoryEntry, File[1m)[0m` and/or its       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         overload writes each POIFS entry to disk using:                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                • `new [1;35mFile[0m[1m([0mparent, [1;35mnode.getName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.trim[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.toPath[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                • Without any sanitization or normalization steps.                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - This allows an attacker-controlled POIFS entry name to perform directory       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         escape.                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Patch Attempt                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - At the top of `POIFSDump.java`, `java.nio.file.Path` was added to the imports. [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - In the first `[1;35mdump[0m[1m([0mDirectoryEntry, File[1m)[0m` method block:                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • After reading the document bytes, the code was replaced with logic that:     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                – Trims the raw entry name.                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                – Replaces all `..` sequences and path separators with underscores to form   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `safeName`.                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                – Constructs `outPath` and `parentPath`, both normalized.                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                – Verifies `[1;35moutPath.startsWith[0m[1m([0mparentPath[1m)[0m`.                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                – Creates any necessary directories.                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                – Opens `[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1m([0moutPath[1m)[0m` to write the data.                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Similar sanitization was added for nested `DirectoryEntry` branches before   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         recursing.                                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                 at [1;35morg.apache.poi.poifs.dev.POIFSDump.main[0m[1m([0mPOIFSDump.jav[1;92ma:80[0m[1m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 at                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.poi.POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1m([0mPOIPOIFSDumpFuzzer.jav[1;92ma:74[0m[1m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         DEDUP_TOKEN: ac6e69a60acc10da                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         == libFuzzer crashing input ==                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         An Apache POI dev tool, `POIFSDump`, was flagged by Jazzer for a file path          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         traversal vulnerability. The fuzzer input contained “..[35m/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m”  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         in an entry name, and the sanitizer halted execution when `Files.newOutputStream`   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         was called on an unvalidated path. A patch was proposed that:                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Introduced `java.nio.file.Path` and normalization checks.                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Replaced occurrences of “..” and path-separator characters in entry names.        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Verified that the resolved output path starts with the intended parent directory. [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Created any missing directories before writing files.                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         When this patch was applied, the build broke with a series of compilation errors    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`illegal start of expression`, expected semicolons, mismatched braces[1m)[0m at the spot [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         where the second overload of `[1;35mdump[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` was redefined, indicating unbalanced or    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         misplaced braces in `POIFSDump.java`.                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. Initial Issue                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Exception reported by Jazzer:                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical:                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                File path traversal: [35m/tmp/.../[0m[95mRoot[0m Entry/..[35m/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Stack trace highlights `FilePathTraversal.checkPath` hooking into              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mPOIFSDump.dump[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`, ultimately calling:                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```java                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              [1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1m([0mnew [1;35mFile[0m[1m([0mparent, [1;35mnode.getName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.trim[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.toPath[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - No sanitization or normalization is performed on `[1;35mnode.getName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`, allowing    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `..` segments to escape `parent`.                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Observations in the Initial Issue                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Both file and directory entries are handled, but neither path is validated.    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Directory creation is attempted via `new [1;35mFile[0m[1m([0mparent, [1;35mentry.getName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m`        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         without path checks.                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The vulnerability is reproducible under fuzzing with malicious entry names.    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Patch Attempt                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Added `import java.nio.file.Path;`                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - In the `[1;35mdump[0m[1m([0mDirectoryEntry, File parent[1m)[0m` method branch for document nodes:   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Trimmed `[1;35mnode.getName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`, replaced `..` with `_`, and stripped path          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         separators.                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Created an output `Path`, normalized it, and verified                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35moutPath.startsWith[0m[1m([0mparentPath[1m)[0m`.                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Ensured parent directories exist via `Files.createDirectories`.              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Wrote bytes via `[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1m([0moutPath[1m)[0m`.                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - In the directory-entry branch:                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Applied the same sanitization to directory names.                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Created the sanitized directory before recursing.                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - In the other `[1;35mdump[0m[1m([0mPOIFSFileSystem, [33m...[0m[1m)[0m` overload:                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Sanitized the `name` parameter identically, normalized its path, checked its [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         prefix, created directories, and opened the output stream on the normalized path.   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. Patch Result and Logs                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Compilation failed in `POIFSDump.java` with ~[1;36m14[0m errors at line [1;36m141[0m [1m([0mthe        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         signature of the second `public static void [1;35mdump[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`[1m)[0m, all indicating “illegal    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         start of expression” or missing `;`.                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The final error “reached end of file while parsing” shows an unmatched closing [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         brace.                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - These errors imply that the patch introduced misaligned or missing braces,     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         causing Java to interpret the method declaration in an invalid context.             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m. Areas for Further Investigation                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `POIFSDump.java` around the modified blocks: verify correct opening/closing    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         braces and that the two `[1;35mdump[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` methods are top-level members of the class.     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Ensure imports and exception declarations align with the existing class        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         structure.                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Review other sinks in the `org.apache.poi.poifs.dev` package for similar       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         unvalidated file writes [1m([0me.g., any utilities that dump OLE2 structures[1m)[0m.            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Examine test harnesses or build scripts to confirm code formatting rules or    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         automated checks that might enforce brace style or method placement.                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
